1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Kubernetes v1beta1 to v1 API Storage Version Registration

## Your Task

Find all Go source files in kubernetes/kubernetes that register API group storage versions mapping v1beta1 to v1 equivalents. Look for REST storage providers (in pkg/registry/) that define both v1beta1Storage() and v1Storage() methods, the StorageVersion manager interface (in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/), and the ResourceEncodingConfig that controls which GroupVersion is used for etcd storage.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the migration domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kubernetes--v1.32.0, sg-evals/client-go--v0.32.0, sg-evals/api--v0.32.0, sg-evals/etcd-io-etcd.

```json
{

  ],

  ],

    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go", "symbol": "FunctionName"}

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

91-assistanttext-
The answer has been written to `/workspace/answer.json`. Here's a summary of the findings:

## REST Storage Providers with both `v1beta1Storage()` and `v1Storage()` methods

Three key files in `pkg/registry/` define both methods:

1. **`pkg/registry/authentication/rest/storage_authentication.go`** — `authentication.k8s.io` group, serving `selfsubjectreviews` in v1alpha1, v1beta1, and v1
2. **`pkg/registry/storage/rest/storage_storage.go`** — `storage.k8s.io` group, `volumeattributesclasses` in v1beta1 + main storage types in v1
3. **`pkg/registry/admissionregistration/rest/storage_apiserver.go`** — `admissionregistration.k8s.io` group, webhook configs in v1, mutating admission policies in v1beta1/v1alpha1

Other registries with versioned storage methods include `resource/rest/storage_resource.go` (v1alpha3 + v1beta1) and `networking/rest/storage_settings.go` (v1alpha1 + v1Storage).

## StorageVersion Manager Interface
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/storageversion/manager.go`** — defines the `Manager` interface with `AddResourceInfo()`, `UpdateStorageVersions()`, `PendingUpdate()`, `LastUpdateError()`, `Completed()`

## ResourceEncodingConfig
- **`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go`** — defines `ResourceEncodingConfig` interface (`StorageEncodingFor`, `InMemoryEncodingFor`) and `DefaultResourceEncodingConfig` implementation

## Storage Version Overrides
- **`pkg/kubeapiserver/default_storage_factory_builder.go`** — `NewStorageFactoryConfig()` explicitly maps resources like `networking/ipaddresses` and `networking/servicecidrs` to v1beta1 etcd storage via `ResourceEncodingOverrides`
